"Allow me to introduce it to Aruji-sama. My Yato no Kami's Divine Raiment is , it's a power to temporarily control other Drag-Ride that it touched."

And then she revealed the true shape of her own Divine Raiment without hesitation.

"It snatch the control of the opponent's Drag-Ride at the area centered on the touched spot, the longer the time of contact is‐the more accurate and powerful the command that can be given out. If I can touch a Drag-Ride for ten second without breaking contact, I will be able to put that Drag-Ride completley under my command."

"In reverse, this controlling power will also disappear the longer time pass while we are separated from you, right?"

Krulcifer calmly stepped forward and interrupted Yoruka's talk.

The Spell Code's letters were already vanishing from the surface of Fafnir's armor.

She must have instantly grasped that fact from comparing her own DragRide with others.

Even in the case that they were touched, if they immediately took distance, Yato no Kami would only be able to control the part that was touched.

Even for example they got controlled, the effect would wear out if they took some time separated from Yato no Kami.

But, even after knowing that weak point, it didn't change the fact that it was a Divine Raiment that was hiding a terrifyingly troublesome ability.

Even if one blocked the opponent's attack, but just from that contact the control of their Drag-Ride would be stolen.

Therefore, they would be burdened with an overwhelming disadvantage at

the point they chose close quarter combat.

And then, there was the godspeed sword handling that Yoruka displayed just now.

"…………"

They couldn't win.

No matter how advantaged they were in term of number, they were near residential area here, because they were restricted in what they could do as to not to involve the civilian, they couldn't act excessively.

(Possibly, other than deciding the match instantly‐there's no other way.)

It would be a gamble if he used Bahamut in his state, but Lux resolved himself and put his hand on his Sword Device once more.

Then‐,

"Oi, what's that sound?"

"Didn't it come from that empty plot? It's really close from here!"

"What are the guards doing? Can't be helped……I'll go call them‐"

Such voices could be heard from the surrounding houses with turned on light.

"Looks like people are coming. Let's stop exposing our hand to each other with this much. My objective of displaying my strength and Yato no Kami's power is already accomplished."

Yoruka casually looked around before suggesting that.

But, Celis who was wearing Lindwurm came forward and pointed her huge lance.

"Are you thinking that you can escape?"

"I have no problem continuing you know? It feels like I will be able to have quite much fun if you are my opponent. But, let me ask you instead. Is it really okay, wasting my consideration like this?"

Yoruka's tone sounded like they were only chatting casually.

However that smile which looked gentle in a glance was filled with terrifyingly overpowering pressure.

"Celis-senpai‐this is"

Lux immediately called out to Celis's back.

This girl called Yoruka didn't care about right and wrong.

If they continued fighting like this, she surely wouldn't have the slightest bit of hesitation to involve the civilian and guard gathering here because of the commotion.

They had to avoid that worst case no matter what.

"……I understand."

After hesitating slightly, Celis backed off. Lisha and others also lowered their weapon following that.

Then Yoruka also lowered her katana and slowly faced Lux again.

"Then, Aruji-sama. I'll be waiting ahead in the capital."

Yoruka flashed a bewitching smile and bowed reverently while still wearing Yato no Kami.

"I will ask about the aforementioned matter once more at that time. Is that‐all right with you?" "Are you……serious?"

Lux took a deep breath and asked with a trembling voice.

"You are planning to fight with the intention to restore Arcadia Empire no matter what?"

"Yes."

Yoruka nodded without hesitation in her expression. Then she suddenly showed a gentle smile.

"If Aruji-sama has no intention for that‐I'm planning to accomplish that even by myself."

Saying that, she turned her back at him, and then she looked back with only her head and continued her words.

"It's truly unfortunate that I am turned down here. But, my feeling that wish to devote my loyalty to Aruji-sama doesn't change at all. To proof that, if Aruji-sama come together with me right now, I'll tell you a secret that I'm putting in reserve. It's a talk of a plan‐that concern the life or death of this country."

"……A, plan?"

Those words that contained concerning implication caused Lux to ask back with dubious face.

"I'm looking forward to it Aruji-sama. The time when I can meet with you again next‐"

But, Yoruka didn't answer Lux's question and slowly walked away.

At the same time the surface of Yato no Kami shined. That frame instantly assimilated into darkness and its figure vanished.

"Is that one of the functions of specially equipped type Drag-Ride

Drake‐the camouflage effect?"

When Celis muttered, Lisha and others who came to her side also made vigilant expression altogether.

"Troublesome. It seems that in battle the camouflage ability's performance will drop drastically, even so‐"

"Right……"

Lux nodded at Krulcifer's muttering.

Under the darkness, if she fought while using camouflage, it would be overwhelmingly disadvantageous for them.

Yoruka was fighting simply‐to show her true strength to Lux.

"So, she is waiting in the capital. Don't tell me, is that girl planning to come out in the international tournament?"

Lisha grumbled that with a displeased expression. In respond Philuffy whispered"I wonder" and she dispelled the armor she was wearing.

Krulcifer who saw that also dispelled her armor and sighed.

"But, that girl doesn't look like the type of person who will joke around. It's a bit concerning regarding that point. Whether it's about her statement that she will appear in front of Lux-kun again, or about that some kind of plan too‐"

"……You're right."

A girl who swore to destroy the new kingdom and succeed the dying will of Arcadia Empire.

Perhaps they would fight her once more in the stage of the capital that was holding the All-Dragon Battle.

Lux took a deep breath and looked up to the sky where the curtain of night had been lowered.

The devilish crescent moon that was tinged with shadow.

That existence that seemed as though it was symbolizing the girl called Yoruka was silently looking down on him.

Part 5

Two hours after Yoruka exited the first city block.

At an abandoned building at the outskirt of Cross Field where there was no sign of people.

Yoruka arrived nearby an aging and crumbling residence that was covered with green moss.

"Have you finished your greeting to the chores loving ruined prince, you murdered pretending to be loyal subject?"

Right after Yoruka dispelled Yato no Kami's armor, a voice mixed with contempt greeted her.

Looking up, there was a robed figure standing on the dilapidated house's roof.

It was the Black Marketer who in these few years had wandered from place to place, selling weapon to various country and secretly maneuvered various incidents.

It was a girl named Hayes who at present was taking the position of Heiburg's military strategist.

Yoruka had finished confirming that this girl and three other people were nearby using the radar that Yato no Kami, a Drake-type Drag-Ride possessed.

"Yes, it's just as I expected, he is a person worthy to be the next emperor. ‐By the way, how is the wound of that right hand? You should take better care with that."

Yoruka told with her voice in exaltation while her lips were forming an arc.

She saw through the wounded hand that Hayes was hiding inside her

sleeve and pointed it out. Was that merely a coincidence?

Or perhaps, could it be her mischief that came from her instinct seeing through that it was a wound given to Hayes from Lux?

"…………"

Either way, Hayes snorted in irritation and looked down on Yoruka with her asymmetrically colored eyes.

"Looks like you've forgotten your debt to me after I finally woke you up from your five years of sleeping underneath that island huh? Even though I have even applied a'Baptism'of different kind from mine into that left eye."

"If that's really the case, then it would be better if only you didn't entrust me to that odd noble and met me right from the start instead to talk about various things."

"……You mean Dobar? That was a miscalculation. I planned to give you instruction through that guy. Because that idiot tried to use you as he pleased, it became problematic. That's all."

"I never thought, that at that time even you were also inside the Ark. If I knew, I would also help. It was a pity."

Hayes glared in annoyance at the jesting Yoruka. She then threw a letter that was sealed with wax to her.

"The plan is written there. Your role until the appointed day is there. Dump it there after you finished reading, and then piss off from my sight quickly."

"I understand. Then let us have a united front just as planned. In order to‐destroy this new kingdom."

Yoruka answered while opening the seal of the letter, after that‐she left without any sound from there.

When the girl's presence completely disappeared, the three shadows lurking in that place silently moved out.

Sania, Egnid, Kirly.

These three people of the special force'Cerberus' who were the direct subordinates of Hayes were Drag-Knights affiliated with Heiburg Republic.

The brown skinned girl Sania who was their leader lifted up her face as though she had been waiting for it.

"Will that woman really move as we intended? Certainly her strength is something unparalleled, but isn't it a bit dangerous using her?"

When Sania advised so with a slightly nervous tone, Hayes sighed and turned her back on her.

And then she slowly turned only her head back while her body was basking on the moonlight of ultramarine color.

"You're nitpicking on my strategy? The likes of you who is at the lowest class in Heiburg is now really a big shot huh."

"…………"

Sania held her tongue after that mocking sentence.

"Hayes-sama. That's……"

The red haired man beside Sania, Egnid reflexively tried to say something, but Sania's hand quickly stopped him.

"We are moving."

At that moment, Hayes looked down on the three with a grin pasted on her face and she told them the answer.

"The preparation is already finished. The Empire's Assassin Dagger and that ruined prince, they will surely try to kill each other following their own will, due to the garbage conviction they have‐and the inevitable incident that will happen in the capital after this. Do I need to explain more than this to you all who are nothing but a single cog in the big picture?"

"No……"

Sania silently answered so toward Hayes who was making a wicked countenance.

If their master had her own thought, then they could only withdraw here.

"After this we will head toward the capital just as planned. Then, excuse us."

After Sania said that, she took only Egnid with her and left.

Before long after the two entered into a plain with no sign of people, the red haired man sighed.

"Fuu……even so, as expected that newcomer strategist-sama is really difficult."

"Don't chatter. We are already formally military personnel."

Sania immediately rebuked Egnid from his grumbling.

"Military personnel eh……. Certainly that's so, but is it really okay for us to keep being like this?"

"What do you mean?"

"I mean, that strategist and also the other, aren't they still hiding something from us?"

Egnid muttered that and slowly looked behind him.

It was as if he was being vigilant against the existences at that direction.

"The other, what do you mean by that?"

"Have you ever seen Kirly's bare face?"

"Never……. I heard that her face had burn mark. She got it when Arcadia Empire invaded her home when she was still a child."

"That was just on the surface don't you think? That girl isn't like us who was taken custody from among the war orphans by Heiburg's military affair department and entered officer training school, she was brought from who know where by that strategist. I heard that she cannot even speak word so the story you heard actually doesn't come directly from her‐. I incidentally, saw that girl's bare face before this."

"So what? Don't tell me, under the mask it was a monster, there's no way that's true."

"Exactly like that."

"…………"

Sania's complexion changed when she heard Egnid's immediate reply.

"Just joking. ‐Wait, don't pull out your sword captain! It's half true!"

"Just speak without putting on air."

"Aah geez, we too have got a position that is a bit respectable now, so let's act with a bit more composure yeah. ……So, about Kirly's bare face‐when she took off her mask and lowered her hood, there was something metallic like a bird's feather attached on her head."

"Bird's, feather?"

"Of course, it wasn't accessory or anything. It looked like it's directly growing from around her ear. What's more, her face is a pretty thing, there ain't any burn mark or anything, not in the slightest yeah."

"Something like sickness, or deformation from birth. And the mask was for hiding that?"

"Who knows. But, regarding that strategist-sama, there is only thing that is clear about her. Do you know?"

"……Even I know if it's just that much."

Sania made a bitter smile that was mixed with resignation and she kept silent.

Both of them became war orphan at the war with the old empire, from there they were at the lowest social strata for a long time before they became military soldier.

Even so they were just Drag-Knight of the lowest class because of the difference of birth. One day they were picked by Hayes who arrived at Heisburg and valued as her direct subordinates‐after that when Hayes was placed as Heisburg's military strategist, they formally obtained a position as a knight within the country.

But, even so they had a feeling that was like a tinge of anxiety, that it was hard to honestly accept their present situation.

The outsider existence called Hayes who was wholly enveloped in mystery.

They wondered whether it was all right to entrust the fate of their country in the hand of such person.

"We don't have any other choice than to settle this."

They had hesitation.

Even so Sania and Egnid renewed their determination that they could only advance forward and they started walking once more.

Chapter 2: The Night Before AllDragon Battle

Part 1

It was the morning two days later after Yoruka appeared in front of Lux and caused a disturbance.

Finally Lux and others departed to the capital for the sake of the international tournament‐the All-Dragon Battle.

Using horse carriage, they passed through four checking stations for three whole days before they finally arrived there.

The royal capital Lordgalia.

After the old empire perished, it was rebuilt. Its name and also townscape were greatly changed and now it was the biggest city of the new kingdom.

The castle town, a metropolis that continued toward the enormous palace was separated into seventeen blocks, far more than Cross Field. Its population density was also high.

So that it was possible for the city to be self-sufficient, industry, agriculture, commerce‐and then army's base were scrupulously laid out, lining up with regularity that was a marvel.

Arcadia Empire that possessed several hundred years of history, all of its technology and assets were massed to build up the workings of this city, even now after five years since the empire turned into the new kingdom, it still remained as scenery.

"It has also been really long since I'm here."

Entering the high class inn of the capital that they reserved, Lisha sat down on the sofa at the entrance and muttered so.

Perhaps because of the long travel, the other selection members entered their allotted room to take some rest it seemed.

"During the summer vacation, it seems there are also a lot of students returning back to their home in the capital(here) you know? It seems they will also come to cheer for us in the All-Dragon Battle, if you're lucky you might cross each other in the city somewhere."

Headmaster Relie who went out of her room stretched her back while saying that. Hearing that, Lux's little sister who was nearby‐Airi was showing a complicated expression.

"Rather than talking about that, it's a wonder that the government people is allowing headmaster to still lead this group."

"……Well, it was just barely. At any rate, on top of getting a scolding of a lifetime's worth, I was also paying quiet a lot of fine. Currently I'm not behind the bar is solely thanks to my current position and money."

"It's not really something that can be joked about though……"

After Lux retorted at Relie who was showing a complicated smile, an awkward atmosphere flowed.

The training camp at Ries Island that was carried out two weeks ago.

There the headmaster Relie performed Ruin investigation without permission from the government in the capital in order to save her little sister Philuffy.

It seemed that her responsibility for that illegal act was questioned and there was a really intense exchange between her and the capital's government.

But, in order to avoid mayhem that could affect the All-Dragon Battle that was approaching close, currently her punishment was put on hold.

For the time being Relie avoided jail with only stern warning given to her temporarily.

"Well, because of that I was made to transport 'that' which was hidden in the academy to here but‐, it's relieving instead that I don't need to manage it more than this."

"'That'?"

Lux reacted to Relie's whisper.

"……Ahaha, it's nothing. Just forget it."

Relie said that with a flustered look along with a stiff wry smile.

Now that she mentioned it‐Saina who came to the academy as a spy from Heiburg was looking for something in the academy. He heard about it from Airi, but was this about that?

"…………"

But, Airi didn't move her gaze from the book she opened. Seeing her behaving that it wasn't any concern of her, Lux too didn't pursue any further.

Then, Relie began to talk to varnish over the awkwardness.

"Rather than that, we're finally in the capital, so how about everyone have fun in this city? There is also a festival that will start soon."

"It's the festival for the new kingdom's nation founding anniversary isn't it?"

When Relie muttered that, Celis who exited from the hotel room interjected lightly.

"It seemed that five years ago it was called the empire's holy birthday festival, but right now various things has changed. Not just that name‐but also the festival's content."

As expected from the daughter of a duke of one of the four great nobles, Celis was knowledgeable in various subjects.

"Actually I should also come along with you kids as the one leading this group, but I'm a bit tired. And so, kids who is still energetic can go for a relaxation before the tournament."

Saying that, Relie took out a whole bundle of paper money from her wallet and put it on Lux's hand.

"Tha, thank you very much. ‐Wait, this is too much you know!? We don't need this much!"

"My, is that so? Well, you can just return it later if there is leftover."

As expected from the heiress of Aingram family that was a prominent conglomerate even in the new kingdom.

That sense of money was completely different from Lux who was doing odd jobs for these five years.

(Or rather, it will be dangerous instead if we are walking around carrying this much money though……)

"Come to think of it, this is my first time coming to the capital. Lux-kun, can I ask you to guide me through the city for a bit?"

While Lux was thinking of such thing, Krulcifer who arrived at the entrance asked him that.

"Ah, okay. I don't mind though‐"

When Lux was about to agree readily like that,

"Oi! Don't decide that as you please! I also have plan to borrow Lux after this!"

Lisha cut in and the usual quarrel began.

"There are also some of you who is tired and don't feel like going out, I'll leave that for you to decide among yourself. But‐it will be standing out if you kids are moving in group, so split yourselves into group with four people at most per group, okay?"

With Relie's suggestion, they made groups using lottery and it was immediately decided.

One group was made of Lux, Lisha, Krulcifer, and Airi.

The other group consisted of Celis, Philuffy, Noct, and Sharis.

Tillfur who usually took initiative in going outside couldn't participate because her condition broke down from the long travel. Saying "Heartless people‐!" she glared resentfully at the other two Triad members.

"We will buy a lot of souvenirs for you."

"Uuu……, don't forget okay?"

Lux consoled his dejected classmate before sallying forth into the capital's city.

Because the time was still afternoon, it seemed there wouldn't be a problem if they didn't go far away.

"……A, right right. The selection members from other country has also come it seems, so do your best to not cause any trouble before the tournament."

Relie said that at the end. Lux and others nodded and exited the inn.

"Then, where should we go first? The place that I want to go first is the

Drag-Ride museum at the capital though."

"As always, you don't change at all aren't you……. Don't you have other interest in this rare chance that we have gone as far until the capital?"

"Muu……. Then try saying what do you want to do!? What do you know when it's your first time here!?"

"Let's see. First there are several tailors that are famous even in the capital nearby from here. There are many other shops too, so just looking around is also not bad. Besides, it will be a bit far but if we go to the national park, there will be a small stream there, it feels like it will be refreshing there. If you feel a little hungry, there is also a street lined up with stalls right there‐the district of craftsman are making and selling things like watch accessories or special handicraft‐"

"Wai, wait a second Krulcifer! Isn't this your first time coming to the capital!?"

Lisha yelled flusteredly toward the girl who was talking continuously without pause.

"What I said just now are courses that are comparatively common when sightseeing in the capital you know? How about you also do a little investigation so that you have something to talk with the other nobles too?"

"Kuh……!? Back at you, you actually don't need any guide right from the start right!? You vulgar girl, that was just your excuse to invite Lux!"

Lisha spontaneously yelled when she saw Krulcifer telling her like that with a cool tone.

She was inadvertently more knowledgeable than Lux who was supposedly living in the capital at the past.

"Then for now, should we leave it to Krulcifer-san?"

As expected, even Airi too didn't seem to be that knowledgeable about the capital's layout. In the end they had fun in the capital's street following Krulcifer's escort.

Part 2

A few hours later.

They went around a lot more places than they expected and by this time the sun had already went down completely.

Lux and others, the four people were taking dinner in a large eatery nearby the main street.

As expected from an eating place that had existed for many years in the capital, the meal was delicious without anything to complain about. The four were reminiscing about their day but‐.

"Oi oi, I beg you lad. Don't sleep in this kind of place! Also you're drinking too much."

When they were thinking to leave soon, they could hear the troubled voice of the owner from the corner.

"Ain't no one is slee‐ping here……. Just shut up and bring more sake here‐. Munya……"

A male was lifting up a wooden beer mug while speaking with a tone that was obviously dead drunk from anyone's point of view.

His age was still young. The young man's trait was his dull blonde forelock that was bristled up as though frayed, and his sanpaku eyes. (TN: Eyes with visible white between the iris and the lower eyelid)

He was wearing durable looking black shirt and trouser.

Within that simple appearance, it was only the rustic silver sword belt on his waist that was standing out.

Looking only from his looks, he looked like a rude thug, but perhaps because of his child-face that had no ill-will in it, he didn't give that bad of an impression.

"To begin with, are you in the age that can drink alcohol huh lad? You look really young."

"It's oka‐y. My principle is 'reckless challenge' yeah……. Being reckless without conservativeness is what gonna open the new path‐uppuh"

"You're over your limit there!? By the way lad, you look like a traveler, but where are you come from?"

"Who care‐s, just pour more drink. After all I cannot drink back home see‐……. I'm told today is a rare festival in the capital yea‐? Don't be so stingy‐"

"The nation founding anniversary is still two more days. ……Rather than that, you look young but do you got money on you?"

When the young man grumbled with bright red face, the owner sighed and asked.

Lisha beside Lux whispered in exasperation while watching that scene from distance.

"I thought that only nobles came to the capital, but there are also quite a lot of country bumpkin huh."

"Your voice is loud you know, princess."

When Krulcifer chided curtly like that, an incident occurred.

"Look here, even like this I got money y'know‐. I earned a lot from my work‐"

The young man took out a wallet from his trouser's pocket. The moment he put it on the table, a middle-aged man drinking alcohol behind him stood up and moved suddenly.

"‐"

Drunkenness reflexively vanished from the young man's expression and his hand reached at his sword's handle.

But, when the middle-aged man reached out at the wallet, the man snatched it in the blink of eye and vanished to outside the restaurant.

After a tense moment, a small commotion filled the restaurant.

"Aah-ah, he got you there lad. That kind of fellow ain't someone you usually find in the capital, but robber who came here in this kind of time from various place y'know."

With a complicated look, the restaurant owner told so to the young man whose wallet was stolen.

"…………"

Lux who had experience doing odd jobs many times at the capital had recollection of it.

Before and after the country founding anniversary or the tournaments including All-Dragon Battle, the population of the capital that was already a lot even under normal circumstances would increase explosively.

Nobles and travelers would gather to watch the event from various places of new kingdom‐or even from the foreign countries.

And then, the robbers would also gather into the capital, aiming for their wallet.

But, the capital was different from Cross Field. Although its size was vast but there was unexpectedly few hiding place there.

The streets were systematic due to the wisdom from the past in order to be able to corner hostile individual and captured them.

"……I'll go for a bit."

Lux pulled back his chair with a clatter and stood up.

"Oi wait, where are you going Lux!? Don't tell me‐"

When Lisha called out in surprise, Lux was rushing out of the restaurant.

"I can predict where the thief will escape in general, so everyone go back first to the inn!"

Lux only said that and then ran out without giving the girls any time to stop him.

Chasing after the man's footsteps and presence, Lux moved from the main street into a complicated back alley.

When he arrived at the end of a gloomy alley some distance away from the bar, he found an unexpected sight there.

"Chih! Someone caught up already, but‐"

The man just now who Lux thought as a mere thief summoned a Wyvern Drag-Ride and wore it.

"-……!"

Because using Drag-Ride in the capital would stand out, this was something that took Lux by surprise.

However, if the thief could escape for the moment to the sky, it would be hard to catch him when he went away from the capital.

"Come, the symbol of power the winged dragon of crest. Obey my sword and take flight, Wyvern"

This is the first time Lux summoned Drag-Ride since he used Over Limit.

His use of Wyvern also doubled as light rehabilitation, but physically it was as though there was no problem at all.

(……I can do this!)

Lux ascertained the sensation of wearing Drag-Ride while flying in pursuit of the thief's flying Wyvern.

The thief held his breath for an instant in order to further accelerate his Drag-Ride.

Lux didn't overlook that opening and he lifted up his Scale Blade, it was then,

"Oi prince, I'll be first okay?"

A voice with a tone that had peculiar mannerism in it came. Along with it, the thief's Wyvern in front of him was struck down.

"……!?"

There an unfamiliar Drag-Ride‐a Drag-Ride with countless scale-like armor attached on it was taking stance with a Blade that was strangely curved.

(This is‐!)

It was a male Divine Drag-Ride user that was rarely seen other than Lux himself.

Because female's aptitude with Drag-Ride was far higher than male, DragKnight that could skillfully use Divine Drag-Ride that was difficult to control and consumed energy intensely was few in number even throughout the world, but‐this young man, even in his completely drunken state, he controlled his Drag-Ride with precision and knocked down the enemy in an instant.

"Gu, gahah……a!"

The knocked down thief writhed from the impact and he didn't look like he could take anymore action.

The blonde young man who saw that was about to deal additional attack below him.

"I'm not gonna kill you cause it'll be troublesome, but I'll at least take both your arms."

The large Blade with strange curve was going to sever the thief's arms from the elbow just as the young man proclaimed, but then‐,

"……!?"

*GIIN!*

The blade was deflected along with a high-pitched metallic sound.

Lux's Scale Blade blocked the Blade that they young man swung down.

"Stop. This person cannot move anymore. More than this is meaningless."

The young man's eyes opened wide for a moment in surprise, but he soon stared at Lux with an ironic wry smile.

"That's really naïve, prince. That line is really unthinkable coming from the survivor of that Arcadia Empire's imperial family that was extolled as inhuman yeah."

Contrary to his words, the young man obediently dispelled his armor and sheathed back his Sword Device into his sword belt.

Because the thief had already fainted, Lux also dispelled his armor next after checking the surrounding vigilantly.

And then, once more Lux faced the young man confronting him still with a smile on his face.

"You know? About me‐"

"You're a bit of celebrity at the neighboring country y'know? Even a slacking guy like me know that much."

"…………"

The young man's sharp gaze caused Lux to tense up his expression too.

Arcadia Empire reached out its hand not only within its vast territory, but also to the surrounding territorial water and island. At the time various skirmishes happened repeatedly with many countries at the surrounding.

There were still many foreign countries that held grudge against the imperial family that was the main culprit of that.

When strange silence and strained atmosphere were flowing between the two‐,

"Oooi! What are you doing, Greifer!"

A bit high soprano voice resounded in the back alley the two were at.

The one who arrived was a young man that was his same age with an androgynous face.

"Aaa-aa. The troublesome guy came……. I'll introduce him, he is my staff officer and also the one tasked wiping my ass, the great Coral-sama."

"What stupid thing you're saying! Just how many times I told you already not to draw your Sword Device inside the capital!?"

The young man who was called Coral yelled angrily at Greifer before turning toward Lux.

"Are you all right Lux!? You are weak right now, that's why forcing yourself is‐"

Lisha and others came running slightly behind, but they stiffened when seeing the duo facing Lux.

"What do we have here, the selection members of the new kingdom is also coming eh. Hey there."

"You two, who are you……"

When Lisha questioned with a slightly tense voice, Greifer showed a sarcastic smile.

"Ain't introducing from yourself the polite thing to do? But yeah certainly,

I ain't this country's person……gofuh!"

*Bam*, Greifer pitched forward due to the strong hit from Coral on his back.

As though to replace him, the young man called Coral moved to stand before Lux and others.

"Please forgive my colleague's rudeness. We are the selection members of

Vanheim Dukedom. Nice to meet all of you."

The young man greeted with a refined voice and gesture. Lux and others faltered for a moment.

"He is our leader, Greifer. My name is Coral. We has only arrived the other day but‐forgive us for causing a ruckus."

It seemed that different from Greifer who had a peculiar personality, this young man named Coral was really amicable.

"We don't need to apologize here Coral. In the first place, I'm just trying to catch the thief stealing my wallet‐"

"It's forbidden to drink alcohol at our expedition destination isn't it, Greifer? I'll tell about this matter to the instructor later. I think that this time won't end up with only training as your punishment, so you better prepare yourself."

"Uwaa!? What are you gonna do if we lose the All-Dragon Battle because of this huh!? Oi Coral! Think again about it‐"

Coral shut the fussing Greifer's mouth with his hand while facing Lux and others once more.

"I'm sorry to bother you, but can I ask everyone to take care of the thief sleeping there?"

Lux took a step forward toward the awkwardly smiling Coral and replied.

"Yes. We will hand him over to the guards. Perhaps that way will be less troublesome in various things."

"Thank you. Well then, we will have to trouble you with that."

"Ah, the wallet……. It was falling there."

"Ah, I'm sorry. But, we've been a bother to everyone, so‐please, I hope everyone can have a nice dinner with this."

Coral said that while taking out several piece of paper money from Greifer's wallet.

"Oi! Don't take out other's money as you please! I didn't say anything about giving‐"

Coral ignored the protesting voice from behind him and offered the money to Lux with a smile, but,

"We didn't do anything, so it's fine. Rather than that, something like this happened out of nowhere, but if you could please not hate the new kingdom because of it……it will make me glad."

Coral's eyes instantly opened wide after hearing Lux's words that were said with a wry smile.

"……It's surprising."

Coral whispered that accompanied with a small admiration.

"Eh……?"

"You are completely different from the imperial family of the old empire that I've been hearing."

Coral said that with a smile. He then held out his right hand toward Lux quietly.

For a moment Lux didn't understand his gesture, but when he understood that it was for handshake, Lux responded. Coral grasped his hand back smilingly.

His androgynous handsome look looked like a girl. Lux felt his heart throbbed slightly.

"……-!?"

Instantly, heat flickered and burned his brain, as though electricity was flowing behind his yes.

His consciousness was getting farther away, as though he was suddenly entering inside a sandstorm.

"……Is something wrong?"

"Ah, no. It's nothing‐"

Lux immediately separated his hand from Coral's right after he spoke to him, and the pain settled down.

Lux wondered just what in the world that was just now.

"Then, let's meet again at the All-Dragon Battle."

Coral brought the talk to finish like that and he took away Greifer from the back alley.

Lux finally breathed out in relieve. At that moment, Lisha who had handed over the fainted thief to the guards quietly arrived in front oh him.

"Oi Lux. You were holding that guy's hand for really long there……I'll say this just in case, that guy just now is a man you know?"

Lisha said that to him with twitching gaze that looked doubtful.

"I, I know that. That much is‐"

"It's unexpected that Lux-kun has interest in that direction. It's no wonder that your reaction is weak against my advance."

"Wai-!? Even Krulcifer-san, just what are you saying!?"

"You're panicking like that make it even more suspicious. Well, putting aside the joke‐they are formidable enemy aren't they?"

Airi concluded like that while taking a final shot at Lux while she was at it.

Lux was also in agreement regarding that.

"Especially that one who was called Greifer, if I remember correctly he is the candidate for 'Seven Dragon Paladin' of Vanheim Dukedom."

"……Seven Dragon Paladin?"

"That kind of talk was suddenly announced while Lux-kun was forced to bed."

When Lux tilted his head in puzzlement hearing those unfamiliar words, Krulcifer quietly taught him what it was about.

"The talk is about forming an organization where every country is cooperating to oppose the threat of Abyss that is increasing every year. About the Seven Dragon Paladin, they are the Drag-Knights where each country will select one person as their representation in that organization."

After hearing the further detail from Airi, it seemed that there was still time until the Seven Dragon Paladin was selected, but there were already several countries that put out their candidate's name.

"That guy's personality is a bit like that but, he looks troublesome huh. ……Rather than that let's go back, I'm sleepy."

"You're right."

Lisha yawned 'fua' with a cute gesture. Lux smiled wryly to that and nodded in agreement.

After that they went back straight to the inn without stopping anywhere and retired to bed.

Part 3

At the territorial waters slight distance away from the new kingdom.

At that place that had a lot of reef and even fishing boat couldn't approach, a huge building was hidden within the cover of fog.

Inside‐countless metal objects were lining up in a spacious space. Several silhouettes were there.

One was a silver haired girl wearing jet black robe‐Hayes.

A blue haired maid was standing at her side, Mishis.

The last was a tall and slender man looking at everything with a distant look, Fugil.

"The entire plan is progressing favorably, but can I ask you to rethink it again, your highness Hayes?"

"……What is?"

When the maid called Mishis addressed her, Hayes responded while still lying prostrated on the round table at the center.

"Certainly its necessary to offer your blood and mind to control the Artifact(Transforming Weapon), but as I thought it's too reckless. Even if bring them down thoroughly until the root, but if your life is‐"

"So what?"

When Hayes responded with a displeased look, Fugil who was standing while leaning on the wall until now walked toward the table at the center.

"She is merely worrying about your highness the imperial princess. At the previous battle, our greatest pawn that is necessary for the 'imperial capital recapture plan'‐the Yggdrasil was defeated. Of course, if we invest our whole war potential, it'll be possible to defeat them even then. But, your highness will be forced to lose a lot of your time as the compensation of that."

"……Oi Fugil. When your parent's enemy die from sickness, can you then laughed it off and get happy with that?"

"Unfortunately, I'm someone without a single relative."

Fugil smoothly answered Hayes's question that was mixed with irritation inside.

But, Hayes ignored that and showed a distorted wicked smile on her lips.

"A low-life like you won't get it, but if it's me that's impossible. What you call revenge has worth only if you do it by your own hand and nobody else. Hiring a hit man to do it? Waiting for chance until he is killed by someone? ‐That's not it, something like that has no value at all. If I don't drag out those guys in front of me by these hands and kill them myself, then it ain't got any meaning at all!"

Hayes's asymmetrically colored eyes snapped wide open and she yelled.

"That's‐"

"Stop there, don't give me any pointless talk. It's a story you cannot possibly understand. For the lowest and worst traitor who cut down all those bunches who can even be called as your blood relative‐"

"…………"

Fugil returned a fearless smile at the words that Hayes spat out.

"……Get it? I won't borrow your hand in my revenge. You just work like slave until you die like usual for the sake of our empire, that's the only compassion that can be given to you who is of that family."

"By your will. Without any doubt, I am an ally of all of you."

Hayes scowled seeing the humble Fugil.

Almost at the same time, the metallic door at the back automatically opened and a girl came in.

It was a girl with ears that looked like bird feather, wearing an unfamiliar outfit.

"The Artifact's activation as well as the tuning of the Divine Drag-Ride is completed, my lord(creator)."

The girl informed with no pause between her words and robotic voice that didn't contain emotion.

"Can it work? Gear Leader El Fajura. That's including the two original special functions that you have."

"It's possible to execute as planned."

After the girl called El Fajura nodded, Hayes's lips crooked into a smile and she stood up.

"I see, then we're moving. In order to accomplish our longstanding desire and retake that."

Hayes reached her hand toward the small half-sphere object at the middle of the round table.

Instantly that half-sphere was tinged with faint light. Lines of light were circulating along the floor and wall like spider web that was spreading from the center.

Right after that, the wall itself fiercely shook and the exterior started moving on the whole.

Part 4

On the other side, the capital at night.

After Lux and co returned to the high class hotel they reserved, the reunited selection members and Airi were called by Relie and everyone gathered at the entrance.

Perhaps because she had received a lot of souvenir, or perhaps because she had rested properly, Tillfur had recovered her liveliness. That was something good but‐.

"Then without delay, let's have Lux-kun announce who is the girls who has worked hard at the training camp the other day and will receive the prize."

"Eh!?"

The very first sentence that Relie spoke out caused Lux's mouth to drop wide open without closing.

It seemed that it was also unexpected for the other girls too, because everyone stiffened simultaneously.

"My, everyone is cold isn't it? Didn't you all work hard at the training camp for this?"

"N, no……, that's, well it's true but"

Even Tillfur who would normally play along with the mood was replying with a somewhat bewildered feeling.

Lux too had completely forgotten about it until now, but certainly there was such promise between him and everyone.

It was a competition between the members who received Lux's individual guidance at the training camp in Ries Island, about who would be the one who could safely complete the assignment given to them.

The first three name who could complete their assignment first would be able to specially make individual request to Lux as their reward, that was the promise (that Relie arbitrarily decided), but‐.

"Actually, the plan was to immediately decide it right after we returned from the training camp, but then Lux-kun was really tired, and the situation also didn't allow it. And so, can I ask you to announce the result here."

"Uu……"

Everyone's gaze gathered on Lux after Relie's words. Lux hesitated to speak.

He reflexively wanted to say "Can I say it later?", but seeing the eyes of the members around him that were filled with expectation and nervousness, it didn't look like he could escape.

He took a deep breath, then he recalled the training scene at the training camp‐and the activity of the girls after they returned to Cross Field.

"Then‐eerr, first is……"

And then he announced the three names after hesitating about it.

Part 5

"Even so, I wonder what kind of business Lux-chi is called for? What's more it's this late at night~."

"Who knows. Well, it's a summon from the government, so it's not something strange I think."

Inside one room in the inn where the members were staying, Tillfur's muttering was answered by Sharis.

The three members of Triad were sitting down together on the bed inside the room that they were sharing while Tillfur who was wearing her sleepwear was tilting her head in puzzlement.

Only a few minutes ago, right after Lux announced the three names who accomplished their assignment, a messenger from the castle arrived at the inn that the selection members were reserving.

Lux and Airi were the ones summoned. The government had an important talk with them.

"However it's unfortunate isn't it? For Tillfur too, even though you worked that hard, you weren't selected as one of the three."

"Uwaaa……don't say it please, it makes me down. The rivals are just too strong……"

Tillfur's expression was clouded from Sharis's consolation and she sighed.

"Yes. ‐But, I did everything I could, Sharis and Tillfur too. I judged that there is nothing for us to feel shame about."

Noct who was reading book quietly whispered that with her expressionless look unchanging.

After the leader Sharis concluded like that in the end, Tillfur and Noct didn't raise anymore voice of complain.
