Sharis suddenly muttered so when she stared at the window outside.

Ahead of her gaze were the lamps of the people living in the capital that were numbered far more compared to Cross Field.

Part 6

"And, to start off. To congratulate this critical juncture that is the fifth year since the founding of the new kingdom, I……haa, I'm tired."

On the other hand, inside another individual room in the inn, Lisha was reading a document.

Because they reserved the inn, they could choose to share room with someone, but Lisha wanted to spend her time alone just for today.

The largish note in Lisha's hand contained the writing for her greeting at the new kingdom's founding anniversary.

Until now LIsha avoided her work as a princess as much as possible, but this time she couldn't do that and she reluctantly consented.

"Even so, just why didn't Lux choose me!? Even though everyday I'm working hard until late at night in order to improve that guy's Bahamut…… geez."

She was dissatisfied that she wasn't chosen among the three names who accomplished Lux's assignment and received the reward to make request, but because Lux had already complied with her selfishness, she also thought that it couldn't be helped.

'Fuu', Lisha leaked out a small sigh and threw herself on the bed wearing her sleepwear.

"It's depressing doing this public greeting. From the start I don't have the awareness as a princess, and yet‐"

Even so, she could run away from the matter and responsibility before her.

"We, well but……to announce about that thing with Lux, as expected, I have to do this greeting huh."

Lisha imagined about that with faintly blushing cheeks before she muttered somewhat brusquely.

She had already received the consent from her stepmother Queen Raffi too.

She heard that half of the capital's consuls were in opposition, but it seemed that it was somehow accepted.

If it went as planned, the founding anniversary the day after tomorrow would become the day where she would officially announce it.

"I can't wait. With this Lux will become my knight."

She whispered as though to test how it sounded and she ruminated the words.

The hapless fate where the existence of old empire stole her position before she was then placed on the seat of the princess of the new kingdom.

Because of that chronology and upbringing, she was unable to familiarize herself with the position as the new kingdom's princess.

The one who saved her from that was none other than a 'man' who she thought as her enemy, the prince of the old empire Lux. That was why it was a mysterious fate at work.

"Besides, he was also considerate to me at the training camp before. He is really kind."

Lisha's lips slackened abruptly. She laid down on the feathers bed and looked up to the ceiling.

"……But that man, he look sincere from a glance, but he is really a pervert. It's a bit uneasy with him only becoming my knight."

Lisha whispered such thing while lightly closing her eyes and thought about Lux.

If she showed some understanding in that area as a 'woman', Lux would

surely feel satisfied wouldn't he?

'Tha, that's‐. Lisha-sama's body, even though it's small statured, but it's feminine and really sexy but still cute, honestly speaking it excited me……'

"……Uwah!? Am I an idiot!? Ju, just what am I thinking, geez!"

After Lisha recalled a past conversation, she yelled with a bright red face and she came back to her senses.

"Come back quickly already, Lux."

Lisha slowly put her hand on her chest while she whispered with her eyes closing.

Part 7

In another different room‐.

Inside that room that was extravagantly decorated typical of a high class hotel, Krulcifer was changing into her sleepwear while combing her hair in front of a mirror.

Because Krulcifer's homeland, the religious country Ymir also participated in the All-Dragon Battle, the maid of Einfolk family, Alterize would also come to this inn. She was already notified of that through a letter.

At the training camp in Ries island, she was instructed by Lux about overcoming her decisive blow insufficiency.

Her highly accurate marksmanship using long distance Rifle, and her offense and defense that was making use of Fafnir's armament and mobility produced a battle style that left no opening.

She was strong enough with just that. Even in the capital's tournament, it could be asserted that there was almost no one who could best Krulcifer. But, she had a weak point. Her attack was light.

She would be fairly in advantage if she could attack the Force Core of enemy's Drag-Ride with her accurate shot, but in real battle it wouldn't go that conveniently.

If she was facing against Drag-Ride that possessed powerful barrier like Azi Dahaka‐or an Abyss that was resistance against ice ability appeared, her offensive option would be severely limited.

She also could handle other weapon like Blade more or less, but that couldn't become her finishing move.

After they returned to the academy, she directly showed Lux the answer to the assignment he gave her. With that she splendidly won the right to make a special request to Lux.

If it was seen just from that, then it was a really good result, but‐,

"This situation, it's not something that I can really be happy about without reserve."

She let out a small sigh and laid down on the bed face up.

She was looking up to the ceiling that was still new without a single stain on it while recalling Lux's statement.

He said that he would become the exclusive knight of the new kingdom's princess, Lizsharte.

"Perhaps, I'm looking at this a bit too naively."

If Lux was formally appointed as Lisha's exclusive knight, he would be repeatedly recruited to Lisha's official business. And depending on the situation, he would be attending Lisha constantly.

Of course, while they were still military cadet who weren't burdened with that much official business, there wouldn't be that much turn for that.

But, she couldn't erase the feeling that the other side had overtaken her by a step.

"I wonder if I too has become bad at keeping up appearances."

Krulcifer smiled wryly while questioning herself.

Lux himself had a complicated circumstance and past that connected the new kingdom and the old empire. Most likely he himself had an objective that he was trying to accomplish.

Just like Krulcifer who wished to know about the true identity of herself who came from the Ruin.

Because of that she was thinking to deepen her relationship with Lux by respecting his will that wanted to become the new kingdom's strength at the present, but‐.

"To be unable to say what I want to do if there is no reason. I too haven't changed."

Krulcifer was deriding herself like that with a cool smile before she woke up.

She was the only human that was discovered inside a Ruin.

She was taken and raised inside other people's family. She was an outsider that was shunned by that family.

That was why she worked hard to be recognized. After that effort ended in vain, she tried to live without relying on anyone, but,

"Perhaps, this is the first time I was able to feel wanting to rely on a person."

She silently whispered so and spread the map of the capital on her desk.

The diligent Krulcifer had already memorized the simple sketch of the area around the block they were currently at, but she was jotting down even more detailed information by hand.

Yesterday she was able to escort Lux and others without hesitation was also the fruit of her hard work of properly doing the preliminary investigation.

"I'm looking forward to the anniversary the day after tomorrow."

She whispered with a voice that no one could hear.

She had already decided the content of the special request she would make to Lux.

Part 8

And then, in further another room, where Philuffy, Celis, and Relie, the three people were sharing room.

There was still empty room in the hotel, but Celis didn't choose a private room and stayed at the same room with Philuffy and Relie. There were several reasons for this.

One, she was asked by Relie herself to be her observer because she had caused trouble last time.

The other reason because Relie was worried about the Abyss factor residing inside Philuffy's body.

About that itself there wasn't any particular problem, but now there was a bigger problem than that.

"This is……a bit troubling."

Celis whispered after opening the letter that was handed from the messenger who arrived just now and confirmed the content.

It was a secret message sent by one of the four great nobles, Celis's father‐Dist Ralgris.

"My, it's rare for someone of your level to be worried? If you're alright with us, then please let us take part in consultation but‐"

Philuffy at the neighboring bed also nodded in response to Relie's statement.

The gaze of Philuffy who lifted up her upper body on the bed was directed on a book page regarding business company.

"N, no, this is, that's……it's about something that I should resolve myself."

Celis answered in panic before her gaze returned to the letter from her father on her bed.

The content of the letter talked about Ralgris house wanting to invite the criminal Lux to their house for once in order to protect his position.

Further than that, the letter also commanded Celis to make use of her relation with Lux in Syvalles to make him associate with Ralgris house in the meeting they would participate in, and also for Celis herself to proactively give Lux guidance.

"Wha, what could this be about? As expected, for me to bring Lux to

Ralgris's house is‐, it make my heart beat fast for some reason."

When Celis unconsciously raised her voice in reaction to that description, Rleie who was sleeping inside the same room twitched in reaction and her complexion changed.

"N, no……. It's nothing at all so……!"

Celis was making excuse with awkward fast-talking while thinking.

(Really, just what could Chichi-ue possibly think……) (TN: Chichi-ue = a more archaic way to call father)

She talked to her father about the case of Lux becoming the member of the academy's raid unit, Syvalles, but this letter's content was slightly strange.

For a noble to invite outsider into their house had quite the meaning.

Especially if the one doing it was one of the four great nobles, for Dist who had brought to her several talk about engagement or marriage interview, to purposefully tell her to bring Lux to their house, it was something unlikely under usual circumstances.

Was he trying to involve Lux into some kind of big trouble?

Or else, could it possibly be‐.

"Tha, that's something that I still cannot permit! Lux still, hasn't taught me a lot about male……. Ce, certainly he is a male that is closest to me but, something like be, betrothal, as expected it's still too‐"

*gata-!* At that moment Relie stood up from her bed with a pale expression.

"That talk‐can you tell me about it in more detail, Celis-san?"

"N, no! Just now is my misunderstanding, so it will help if you can forget about it for me!"

Celis made excuse in panic, but Relie showed a twitching smile and sighed deeply.

"……I see. No matter how dull Celis-san is in regard of love, but I've been a bit careless. And, what are you going to do about your request toward Luxkun?"

Relie suddenly questioned like that. In respond Celis was,

"Fo, for now, I have to consult about a certain matter to Lux so, that's‐I'm thinking to ask him to make some time at the recess day of the

All-Dragon Battle."

"I see‐the All-Dragon Battle's recess, that means the new kingdom's founding anniversary. At that day, you will go in a date with Lux while progressing the talk until betrothal. What a really terrifying plan……!"

"Just what are you talking about headmaster!? It's not like I‐"

Relie whose thought was heated up even more from hearing Celis's plan was walking to the front of Philuffy who was already looking sleepy.

"Phi. Until now I was preparing an environment that was like in the past for you and Lux-kun so that you two can slowly deepen your relationship while expecting Lux-kun to commit a mistake, but‐now that it has come to this there is no other way."

"Headmaster, just now, it feels like I was hearing strange words that are terribly unwholesome though……?"

Celis retorted with a complicated look, but Relie didn't pay it any mind and called out to Philuffy.

"I wonder what should you ask Lux-kun for with the special request? Preparing an environment where you can approach him more proactively is‐"

"Onee-chan. Noisy."

Relie stiffened into a statue hearing the sudden word that Philuffy whispered with her unchanging serious look.

Philuffy's tone was indifferent like usual, so it didn't sound like she was particularly angry, but as expected Relie still received a shock.

"I, I'm sorry Phi. But, it's not like I want to trouble you and Lux-kun. Rather it's, I want to help just for a bit, for the sake of the future of you

two‐"

"I, already decided, my request to Lu-chan."

Her expression and tone were absentminded like usual.

However, she asserted so without any hesitation. After that Philuffy's gaze dropped to the book once more.

"Phi. You've grown……"

Perhaps sensing something from Philuffy's attitude, Relie stared at Philuffy deeply moved.

"How should I say it, I wish to be permitted to move to another room

tomorrow……"

Celis also took a deep breath after watching that scene with a complicated expression.

"Date, is it……. That, I heard that it is something man and woman will do before marriage but……. Walking with a man just the two of us in the city, as I thought, that will make me nervous."

Celis averted her face from Relie and Philuffy and whispered softly so that she wouldn't be heard.

The young man who saved her by removing the shackle that was the sin and righteousness she was burdened with.

Because of Relie's misunderstanding, the thinking of 'what if' was accelerating inside her mind on its own accord.

(A, as I thought this thinking isn't wholesome‐it's not permitted.)

Imagining herself having a date with Lux, Celis covered her own lips in panic with her sheet.

Part 9

Around the same time.

While the girls were thinking about what they should do with the reward of special request‐Lux and Airi passed through the castle gate and stepped inside the castle.

The hustle and bustle of people remained in the night air in preparation for the All-Dragon Battle that would start tomorrow and the new kingdom's founding anniversary the day after that.

Lux was wrapped with strange nervousness when he entered inside the castle after almost five years.

The chalk white structure that were inherited from the building since the era of old empire was this country's government office.

Inside the spacious assembly hall that was illuminated by lamp's lighting, a great number of consuls were already assembled.

The seating was placed to left and right in stair shape. A red carpet was laid down on the pathway.

Lux and Airi were standing on a platform at the lowest level‐where they were stared down from the stair model seating facing them.

"You must be tired from the long travel, former Arcadia Empire's seventh imperial prince Lux Arcadia. And then his little sister Airi Arcadia."

"We have arrived in accordance to the invitation."

Lux responded like that to the consuls addressing him and bowed.

Their seating was enveloped in ultramarine colored darkness. From where Lux was standing, he couldn't see the face of everyone there.

Originally their face should be visible. But for Lux who was completely distant from the capital after the founding of the new kingdom, he didn't even know most of their face and name.

"So, what business do you have with us?"

Airi who was behind Lux asked the question with a voice that was slightly tinged with nervousness.

The messenger who came to their inn before this only told them 'It's an important talk'.

At that point it was undeniable that it was suspicious, but seeing this many consuls gathering like this, that suspicion turned into conviction.

"What a hasty young lady. ‐Well, certainly it's the night before the AllDragon Battle, it will be pitiful to make you accompany us for a long talk. Oi, prime minister-dono."

The one who urged on with such large voice was a big man with red hair, one of the four great nobles, a man called Bugriser.

Even Lux who wasn't that knowledgeable about the politic in the new kingdom recognized the four great nobles' feudal lords who controlled the vast territory in the four directions since the era of the old empire.

Even their personality and their way of doing thing.

"Do you remember my face? I'm the prime minister who serves as the aide of her majesty the queen, Nulph. We are expressly summoning the two of you here like this is just as you suspected, because we wish you to listen to an important matter that still cannot be disclosed to the people of this country.

'Imperial capital recapture plan'‐it's the plot of Heiburg Republic."

"……-!?"

Lux and Airi's expression changed from Prime Minister Nulph's words.

"A notice has come from the spy we sent to Heiburg, we understand the specific of the plan. It seems that the enlarged military division of Heiburg will enforce it. The plan will be carried out before long‐perhaps even right after the end of this All-Dragon Battle. They will take advantage of the opening when the security of the new kingdom will be short of hand." Nulph was reading from the document on his hand dispassionately.

"But, Heiburg's troops won't attack directly. The remnants who sought asylum there and wished for the restoration of Arcadia Empire‐the rebel army will become the ringleader at the surface."

"The rebel army that escaped to Heiburg will come attacking the new kingdom. So that means, don't tell me……"

Airi whispered with a trembling voice. Prime Minister Nulph nodded silently to that.

"It's just as you surmised. If Heiburg's pet, the rebel army take down the capital, it will become the start of the indirect rule of Heiburg's military division. That's the only thing that we have to avoid at all cost."

The remnants of the old empire.

In other words this was the rebel army's imperial capital recapture plan against the new kingdom.

Their objective was to destroy the pillar of the new kingdom and then bloomed a second time as ruler once more, but they were actually being used by Heiburg Republic's military division to invade the new kingdom.

Furthermore it was obvious that the Black Marketer Hayes was deeply involved in this.

"The supreme commander of the rebel army that became Heiburg's pawn is, a man called Ragreed Forus I believe?"

"Eh?"

A hoarse voice abruptly came from the edge of the parliamentary seat.

The owner of that voice was one of the four great nobles, Zagha Schultzed. Lux reacted to the words he said.

Ragreed Forus.

He was once a high noble that was in the empire faction, a man who was the best friend of Lux's older brother Abel.

And then, he was also the man who once attempted to make Philuffy into a scapegoat at the imperial court.

Five years ago when the old empire perished, his whereabouts became unknown, but to think he was escaping to Heiburg‐.

"Oo, come to think of it, Lux-dono, if I remember correctly‐you were acquainted with him I believe? At the surface he is the leader of the rebel army, but it seems he is the one leading the whole army to attack here you know?"

The destiny between him with Ragreed Forus from their childhood.

The man who inherited the ideology of the old empire markedly appeared leading the rebel army as the supreme commander of the imperial capital recapture plan.

But rather than that information itself, it was the fact that this information was told to him right now in this place that made him sensed a certain omen.

"And……what do you want me to do?"

"Hohou. As expected from a former prince, although you were estranged from politic for five years already, but you possess a profound discernment.

Have you predicted it from what we said just now?"

"You ought to stop with the foolish preface, Lord Zagha."

The voice of a gentleman in the prime of his life interrupted Zagha who was letting out admiration while continuing.

One of the four great nobles, Dist Ralgris.

He is the father of Syvalles's captain, Celis.

"Just as we explained, this country is in the verge of unprecedented danger. In order to prevent that, we wish to borrow your strength, as the trump card against the imperial capital recapture plan."

"What kind of role I'll have more specifically?"

Lux replied shortly and waited for the answer. Dist paused shortly before continuing the talk.

"I have heard about your true strength and deeds of arms from my daughter. Yes, of course I knew about the rumor from the royal capital's tournament(official mock battle), but I never thought that your strength is to the degree of being able to repulse Ragnarok."

"…………"

Lux responded to that with silence.

At first glance it was a compliment to him, but he couldn't get carried away and said anything unnecessary.

The matter of a seed of Abyss was inserted into Philuffy's body and that the seed's host, Yggdrasil had been defeated were significant secrets that were only know to Lux and co.

Abyss was subjugation target by law. That law applied not just in the new kingdom, but anywhere.

Therefore, he absolutely had to avoid from saying anything careless and caused the secret to become known.

"Other than that, I also heard the report that you saved the students many times from Abyss's assault to the academy, and you were victorious against Lord Barzeride in an one-on-one duel. There is already no doubt that you are a prominent Drag-Knight even among the men of the new kingdom. ‐Therefore, we judged that it is possible if it's you."

Dist stopped his calm praising words and changed his tone into a strict one.

"From the scout's report, a hundred Abyss that appears to be the battle strength for the sake of this imperial capital recapture plan are already hiding in an abandoned village northwest from this royal capital."

"……Wha-!?"

That terrifying information that was said really naturally caused Lux and Airi's body to tremble in shock.

Even just several Abyss were hiding strength that could easily destroy a single village without Drag-Ride to oppose them.

If several dozen Abyss were rampaging in the capital unchecked, it would brought danger of destruction in one night just from that.

"Is that information‐true?"

"For the Abysses to quietly lurking in an abandoned village, there is no doubt that the treasure called 'horn flute' that was used by a rebel army's commanding officer you once brought down is in use here. The execution day of the imperial capital recapture plan will be the next day after the end of the All-Dragon Battle. It's necessary for us to be a step ahead of the rebel army and exterminated the Abysses before they can be used to attack here.

Therefore‐"

Dist cut off his words for a moment and gazed at Lux, then, he told him.

"Lux Arcadia. We will have you to take on the role as the decoy to lure all one hundred Abyss."

"……!?"

"Ple, please stop with the joke Lord Dist! That's impossible! No matter how, for my brother alone to face such large army is‐"

Airi pleaded in panic right after Lux held his breath.

But, all the consuls including Dist resumed the talk as though nothing happened.

"We have sent a scout to the abandoned village and confirmed that fact. This role can only be carried out by you, the Weakest Undefeated‐the one who excelled in defense more than any Drag-Knight. And then of course, we don't intent to leave it to you to annihilate all of the Abysses. You will lure the Abysses until a hidden fortress located at the north of the new kingdom, then the army unit standing by there will strike down the Abysses with concentrated fire. That's the plan."

"…………"

"This plan didn't come from my own discretion. It's a conclusion that was hammered in a war council that reflected the opinion of her majesty the queen and all the consuls here. The execution of this mission will be the next morning after the founding anniversary. We will crush the Abyss swarm that is the keystone of the rebel army's tactic beforehand. Also in order to avoid chaos from the foreign countries and the people, refrain from saying a word of this to other people."

'I see', Lux comprehended inside his heart.

It was unclear whether these people had grasped as far until the matter of 'Black Hero', but Lux understood several things.

Putting aside the intention of the four great nobles, the consuls of the new kingdom were putting their utmost trust in Lux's strength, on top of that‐they wished to make the annihilation of the Abysses as the achievement of the new kingdom's army, that was their thinking.

Lux was selected to take the decoy role for that reason.

Arcadia Empire lost the majority of their Drag-Knight's war potential from the coup d'etat five years ago and their military strength was greatly weakened.

The new kingdom was hastening the nurture of the Drag-Knight, but as expected, looking at the whole, it was the fact that there was a large gap opened between the new kingdom's force and the surrounding large countries.

There, they wanted to use this chance where many important people from various neighboring countries were gathering to demonstrate the new kingdom's strength to the people and all other countries.

However, skilled Drag-Knight whou could carry out the decoy role was few in number in the new kingdom, and no one wanted to lose their own superior pawn.

They were trying to use Lux was most likely because of such reason.

"If you cooperate with us, the matter of the other day‐the unauthorized Ruin investigation by the arbitrary judgment of the headmaster of the royal officer academy you are attending, Relie Aingram, as well as the indiscretion of all of you Syvalles who was going along with it in order to save her. We won't question those any further. I think that this is not a bad deal, but what do you think?"

"That's reckless Lord Dist! My brother's wound is still not fully healed for battle. Carrying out that mission by himself is‐"

Airi raised her objection against Dist's offer.

But,

"I understand. I'll do it."

Lux calmed his breathing in only a moment and clearly answered like that.

"Nii-san!?"

"It's fine Airi."

Lux smiled gently in order to calm the worried Airi.

"In the end, this is something that someone has to do. Even the current me will manage somehow, surely."

"…………"

Airi faltered to say further from working her thought to think of various things. Then more voice came from the parliamentary seat.

"Looks like the talk is finished. Then, I'll speak another demand from us."

"Eh……?"

The words of one of the four great nobles Zagha that suddenly came caused Airi to knit her eyebrows. The aged man then grinned smugly and raised four of his fingers.

"Four win‐. In order to obtain enough Ruin investigation right, we want you to get at least four win. Of course, carrying out the aforementioned decoy role is your top priority still."

"……What could you mean by that?"

When Airi made a dubious face, Zagha's narrow eyes narrowed further and he chuckled with a stifled voice.

At the All-Dragon Battle, it would be a round-robin event against each country. This time a total of six battles would be carried out.

In the recent years, the military cadet of each country had grown in strength quite much. Obtaining four victories there was next to impossible.

Nothing could be done about it with just Lux's strength alone but‐.

"It means exactly like how the words sound. It will take some effort to not question the incident we mentioned just now. There is also no way we can just not question the incident of using the Ruin investigation right without authorization itself. Don't worry, I heard that all of you the selection members of Syvalles are a gathering of powerful people. It will be easy to raise four win in the All-Dragon Battle I'm sure. If needs be, you the Weakest Undefeated can just fight hard for the sake of victory."

"That's, no matter what it's too high-handed‐……-!?"

Airi moaned and she prepared to protest further, but her mouth closed against the cold gaze from the consuls that were looking down from the surrounding seat.

The demand of firm promise for obtaining four win in the All-Dragon Battles following the matter of the decoy role.

Lux who had seen the way the old empire did thing in the past could easily read their intention of intentionally forcing difficult tasks to him.

They were preparing a difficult problem that was hard to accomplish in addition of the decoy role matter was so that in the case he was unable to accomplish one of the tasks, they intended to force another troublesome request to him again someday in the future.

They would use this chance to ascertain whether Lux was an existence that was easy to control for the new kingdom or not, and whether he was a beneficial personnel or not. If possible they would want to put a collar on him.

Not a shred of guilt could be seen from such people was because Lux and Airi were criminal from the old empire.

(Aa, this again……)

It was pointless no matter what they said, they who were an existence with weak position.

People like them who held authority would be endlessly self-assured against such weak existence.

Just like the old empire that once imposed tyrannical rule to the people and brought the tide of male chauvinism in the past‐.

(Eh? Just now, what did I……?)

Lux asked himself in his mind because of the strange déjà vu.

It was strange. Even though here wasn't the old empire anymore……why?

But if that was the case‐if it was the same like in the past, then it was easy to understand.

If it was the current him, he had even more way to do thing than in the past.

"Understood. Regarding the decoy role for the Abyss extermination and the four win from the All-Dragon Battle. I will undertake both of them."

"Oo!"

At that moment, cheers and small applause welled up from the stair-shaped parliamentary seat.

Airi looked like she wanted to say something, but after a few moments she hung her head down in resignation.

Part 10

"It became later than we thought isn't it? It's lucky that the rain isn't strong

though‐"

A light rain was gently falling on the capital's townscape.

Countless orange colored lamp colored the scenery brilliantly. Lux and Airi were watching that wondrously beautiful sight while going back to the inn.

After that, there was the briefing session about the detail of the mission where Lux would serve as decoy. He was talking with the military officers about the procedure, terrain information, how to deal with unexpected situation, and so on.

Among those he was a bit concerned about the information which said that Heiburg's Ruin was gone from sight, but it was something that wasn't really related with the operation this time, so even when asked for more detail about it there wasn't any more information.

It would worry him if he made Airi went home alone at night, so he made her waited for long, but when it came to that Airi‐.

"Haa……"

Like that, since some time ago she only kept sighing with a depressed expression.

"How about wearing this if it's cold? I also brought a coat just in case though‐"

"That's not it! I'm not cold anywhere! I'm worrying about Nii-san here you know!?"

Airi said that with a loud voice that was unusual for her. But after that she suddenly returned to her senses and shut her mouth.

Perhaps she was embarrassed about her loud voice, her cheeks were slightly reddening. She averted her gaze and resumed walking.

"Thank you for worrying about me. But, I'm fine. If it's about me‐"

"At that time, why didn't Nii-san say that you cannot use Bahamut……"

Airi showed her back toward Lux who stopped his feet and asked that while walking ahead.

"……I understand. If they don't know about the matter of the Black Hero, then we cannot disclose it intentionally. But, if it's Nii-san then you know aren't you? The meaning, of what I'm saying‐"

And then, Airi stood still and turned around to stare at Lux.

Due to the recoil of using Over Limit, Lux experienced extreme fatigue and burden.

He was recovered until a state where he could use Drag-Ride once more was only a few days ago.

In Airi's calculation, he could only use Bahamut for twelve minutes during the period of All-Dragon Battle.

If Lux used Wyvern, he could use it continuously to a certain degree, but even so it was unclear whether he could serve as a decoy against a large army of Abysses by himself.

"The meaning is different you know? Having only a Wyvern to lure the enemy while continuously escaping, and having Bahamut in reserve so that if I feel like it I can use it to escape while defeating Abyss are two different things‐"

No matter even if he had the Scale Blade that Lisha developed, it was impossible to continuously execute the counter technique Critical Hit when he was surrounded by a large number.

Also, because the situation would greatly vary depending on the number

and variety of the Abyss, he would have to deal with many kind of diverse offense. Dealing with that would surely fray his nerves.

Most of the consuls were taking an optimistic view because they heard that Lux had taken part in Ragnarok extermination, but the matter wasn't that simple.

"Besides, there is the promise that we will obtain four win in the AllDragon Battle too‐the fact is that Nii-san who will carry out the decoy role will become unable to go out in the second half of the match where your appearance is scheduled, and yet forcing that kind of demand is……"

Airi whispered with a grieving expression. Lux floated an apologetic smile toward such Airi.

"Even so, as I thought, I think that it's something that I should do." In the end, it was like that.

The consuls forced a difficult problem on him, but their strategy and decision themselves weren't mistaken.

Using decoy would end it with the minimum death and wounded from the military and made it easier to annihilate the Abysses.

And then, if Lux rejected it, then someone else would have to do it in his place.

Rather than having Lisha or Celis, or perhaps Philuffy to become the candidate for such role, doing it himself let him felt more at ease.

Lux and Airi walked side by side. From the main road they entered into a narrow street where there wasn't any sign of people.

Because of the night's darkness and the rain, the light and temperature at the surrounding suddenly felt like they were dropping drastically.

"……Haa, in the end it turned out like this. If I at least can come along, I will be able to protect Nii-san a little, that was what I thought when coming here but‐"

Airi whispered in melancholy.

However, Lux's body moved reflexively faster than he could reply at her words.

"Watch out-!"

"Kyah……!?"

Lux quickly pushed down Airi who was walking in front of him down on the street's stone paving.

Lux covered the back of Airi's head with his hand so it wouldn't hit the ground but,

"Wha, what are you doing all of sudden!?"

Right after Airi who was pushed down as though being embraced yelled that, the sound of a violent cutting wind was passing through in high speed right above Lux and Airi who were ducking down.

Airi who saw that became speechless and her body froze.

The raining royal capital at night with no presence of people.

A dragon of atypical shape was floating at the air above that street.

"My ba-ad, getting in the way of your fun date like this."

"You are……, from the afternoon‐"

The dull colored hair with a part of the bangs standing on end, and dangerous sanpaku eyes.

A selection member of Wanheim Principality, and one of the candidates for the Seven Dragon Paladin, Greifer.

His tone and attitude was lackadaisical like usual, but his presence was clearly different from before. He was emitting a definite hostility toward Lux and Airi.

"What is your intention?"

"That's my line y'know? Don't play dumb and handover the culprit already. If you do that then I too won't need to attack you."

Greifer was saying strange thing in response to Lux's question.

"What are you talking about!? We didn't do any‐"

"Eh……!?"

Lux and Airi raised a bewildered voice hearing Greifer's words.

"I also saw the new kingdom's crest so it ain't a mistake yeah? It was a Drake-type and he escaped right away, but without a doubt our student was assaulted in a surprise attack."

One Drag-Knight who was serving as guard of the new kingdom was ambushing the representative student of other country.

Such thing should be impossible.

But, looking at the Greifer in front of them who was looking dangerous, it didn't look like he was lying at all.

"The attack was using Breath Gun from long range, so fortunately it wasn't fatal yeah. But both his legs were broken, it was hopeless that he'd make it for the match tomorrow. I'm gonna have you settle the bill for that. Any objection?"

"Don't play dumb this late. Fundamentally any representative of other country don't know anything like where are we staying y'know? Except you new kingdom bunches who assigned the inn for us to stay."

"……Kuh."

'This is bad', thinking that, Lux resolved himself in his heart.

The truth of the incident was completely shrouded in mystery, but the point Greifer mentioned was indeed correct. It was obvious that Greifer had no intention of backing away. Then,

"Come, the symbol of power the winged dragon of crest. Obey my sword and take flight, Wyvern!"

Lux quickly pulled out his Sword Device from its sheath and summoned Wyvern in front of him.

The moment Airi yelled, the two Drag-Rides moved at the same time.

Lux's Wyvern slashed up while flying and Cuelebre descended rapidly while its Blade stabbed downward. The two weapons collided and sharp sound of blade clashing and sparks scattered.

"Airi! Return to our inn and tell Relie-san about this matter, confirm about the mentioned guard! I'll stop him here alone."

"Nii-san-!?"

Airi yelled seeing Lux raising his voice with unusual tension in it.

After telling her that, Lux lightly glided and fixed his posture midair.

Right after the momentary clash, the shoulder armor of Lux's Wyvern was shallowly gouged.

(This is, bad‐)

Even if the fact that Lux wasn't in full health was taken away, this man called Greifer was considerably skilled.

There were two reasons why Lux didn't request Airi to ask for help from Divine Drag-Knight user like Lisha and others.

One, in order to prevent this incident from turning big.

And then the other reason was because he understood that this was an opponent that might harm even Lisha and co.

In that case there was no way Lux could call for help from them here.

"You've got it in you huh, former prince-sama. Defending against my sword with a mere general purpose Drag-Ride, not just that, you even shift the trajectory of my rush so that your little sis won't get dragged into this.

But"

Greifer readied his large Blade‐a weirdly shaped blade with the length of its blade reaching around two mel. Then he circulated the energy from his Force Core through it.

"If you think that this is me being serious, then that will concern my honor yeah."

The air was thick with tension that felt like it was electrifying the skin.

The moment the tension heightened until the limit, Cuelebre moved.

Cuelebre was clad in violent gale that was visible with naked eye and charged forward like a bullet.

At the same time a slash that was several level faster than before drew an arc and assaulted the Wyvern, it was then‐that long blade shined faintly and its length extended several times over.

"Wha-……!?"

The weapon transformed in the middle of slashing.

It was most likely‐Cuelebre's special armament.

The Scale Blade couldn't make it in time to block the attack from the midway transformation that suddenly occurred.

Greifer's Blade was falling toward the Wyvern's shoulder by grazing the Blade Lux was holding, it was then‐,

"Nn?"

*PAAN!* A whirling air burst in front of their eyes and both of them were sent flying backward.

Right after their blades clashed at the beginning, Lux amassed energy in advance to use Howling Howl for holding back the opponent. He immediately released it just now and barely blocked a direct hit on his self.

But, Greifer who fixed his balance in only a single instant didn't pause and pursued after Lux who was attempting to escape to the opposite direction using the momentum of Howling Howl.

The townscape of the royal capital consisted of countless high and low buildings packed close to each other.

One wrong step and they would crash. In such situation, the two skillfully weaved through the buildings and flew in high speed.

"So you dodged my at first sight. Looks like it ain't that much of an exaggeration that they called your defense unrivaled huh."

Greifer smiled fearlessly while driving his Cuelebre and unleashed an attack toward Lux who was intently retreating to take some distance.

"Kuh……!?"

Lux was called as the Weakest Undefeated because he carried out many mock battle in the capital by devoting himself to defense, but the attack of this young man called Greifer was terribly hard to see through.

The sharp slash of the Tail Blade that could transform its range and trajectory midway, and Greifer's timing in throwing Dagger the moment Lux reacted to it was superb. It couldn't be dealt with by ordinary means.

Lux was also holding back the opponent using Howling Howl and Breath Gun, but just a bit of attack didn't even budge Cuelebre that possessed solid armor and barrier.

Therefore Lux couldn't exchange attack with the opponent equally and he was forced to a one-sided defensive battle.

In a glance, Greafer's offensive was just a simple brute force but‐there was no pause between his attacks.

If there was a building at Lux's right side, Greifer would deal out a slash from the left. He limited the escape path, and on top of that he also threw a Dagger as extra attack.

If Lux dodged just barely, Greifer would use Breath Gun and Cannon in conjunction and stopped him in his track.

It was attacking in waves like a storm.

It was like how a skilled hunter would cut the escape paths of his prey one by one, controlling the prey's movement while chasing after it, cornering the prey with certainty.

At first Lux could perfectly dodge Greifer's attack, but the number and power of the attacks were gradually increasing. The barrier of the Wyvern was gradually pierced and the surface of its armor was starting to get scratched.

"You're using a rare Blade there but‐it'd be better for your health if you aren't stingy y'know? In two or three more attacks, I'm gonna chop you up." Greifer's Blade struck down vertically along with that declaration.

But when Lux was blown away backward, Greifer noticed something odd and stopped moving.

"……Hm? This place, where in‐?"

There were few lighting around and the air was quiet like a lake surface.

It was the new block of the royal capital‐the redeveloped district.

It was a place where there would be a lot of construction worker, but at night it was mostly an empty lot.

Lux was estranged with the terrain of the capital these days, but he executed his plan by relying on his memory of the capital's map that he saw when he was summoned just now.

"I see, so you made a show like you are getting cornered while it's actually you who are luring me in? Into this place where it's okay even if we rampage a bit."

Greifer who grasped Lux's plan grinned and readied his sword.

"Man, that's terrifying yeah. A guy who can match me this far by using general purpose Drag-Ride ain't that many even at Wanheim Principality. That's why it's a pity‐that I'm gonna have to crush you here."

Suddenly Greifer's atmosphere changed with his tone and expression looked arrogant.

He used his empty left hand to pull out his Sword Device, held it as though

he was sending thought to it, and then he returned it into the sheath once more.

It was a Drag-Ride control motion to sharpen one's nerve for the mind control operation.

(No good‐don't tell me, he is planning to use Divine Raiment!?)

Greifer sent a piercing eye glint toward Lux's Wyvern, and then he held aloft his Tail Blade really high that the sword blade couldn't be seen from the front.

"It's too late even if you notice it this late y'know, Weakest Undefeated!"

Lux who felt the alarming sign jumped back. At that moment, Greifer threw three Daggers and cut the escape path to the back while he charged forward.

"Kuh……!"

Greifer had anticipated that Lux would take distance by moving backward, and on top of that he accelerated extremely by predicting that escape trajectory.

Normally, Lux's style was to see through the preliminary movement of the enemy's attack and, but now his action to move at a spacious place where he had breathing room in order to neutralize the opponent's initial speed and power was aimed at by Greifer.

In other words, this man called Greifer had predicted Lux's defensive action.

An opening would be created if he deflected the Dagger using his Blade.

Therefore, the moment he deflected the Dagger using Howling Howl, Greifer circled to right beside Lux.

"This is my win yeah? Prince-sama]

He swung the quickly transforming multi-joint blade, aiming at Lux's torso.

But at that moment, Lux who should be taken by surprise met the tip of that blade precisely with the tip of his Scale Blade.

Lux's movement that looked like his escape was cut off was a bluff to entice Greifer into a narrow place.

Lux deliberately got cornered into a place that was surrounded by building to limit the angle of attack of his opponent so he could aim for a counter using Critical Hit.

The perfect timing.

The tip of the Tail Blade that extended out in order to aim for Lux, just when Lux thought he would be able to destroy it completely,

""

"……!?"

The moment both weapons crossed, Cuelebre's whole body was enveloped in blazing light.

Immediately after, the Scale Blade's barrier that Lux generated rebounded from the light and Lux was blown backward.

"U, ah……!?"

Lux who was blown away while rolling on the ground crashed onto a huge clock tower.

He didn't receive lethal wound, but impact ran through the flying device on his Wyvern's back wings. Letters of light floated in front of his eyes, displaying the decreasing output.

(Damn it……! I cannot avoid‐the next attack.)

Lux immediately laid out a barrage of Breath Gun, and he further threw Daggers to hold back the opponent.

But, both attacks were easily deflected by the light enveloping Cuelebre and lost their effect.

"This is‐, that Drag-Ride's Divine Raiment……!?"

Deflecting the opponent's attack‐even the barrier of normal Drag-Ride could possibly achieve such feat, but normally if a Drag-Ride's barrier blocked an attack, it would result in some amount a backlash for the DragRide.

But, that blazing light which was enveloping the armor didn't cause any backlash for the user.

"Correct answer. The ability of Cuelebre's Divine Raiment is 'invicibility'. In a state where I am enveloped by this light, all kind of attacks woulda get deflected, what's more I'm the only one who can attack one-sidedly. I'm teaching you that after all your effort‐that's the prize for fighting me until this far with just a mere general purpose Wyvern."

"Ku……"

Lux groaned. Right after that, the light enveloping Cuelebre vanished as thought it had burned out.

It seemed that invincibility could only be maintained for just around few seconds, but for the current Lux, he couldn't hold out even if the enemy didn't have that.

(Even though I cannot use Bahamut here‐)

"Killing you will make it troublesome later so I'm not gonna kill you, but

I'll have you meet the same fate like my comrade whose legs were broken!"

Greifer lifted up his Tail Blade to aim at Lux who was buried under rubble, but then,

*BASHII-!* A Wire Tail(Dragon Tail Rope Wire) stretching from behind entangled that one hand and stopped it.

"That's as far as you go, Greifer!"

The true identity of the intruder became clear along with that refined soprano voice.

Behind Cuelebre there was the silhouette of an EX Wyvern before anyone noticed it.

The Drag-Knight clad in armor was the young man with androgynous face that was with Greifer before, Coral.

He wasn't wearing pilot suit but the uniform of his own school must be because he was hurriedly rushing to here.

"Please forgive his rudeness. Our leader ran by himself‐"

"Oi, why are you stopping me? And then what are you doing apologizing as you please huh, Coral? What I'm doing here is a justified revenge y'know?"

"Did you see him as the one actually doing it? If not then there is no proof at all. As long as the culprit isn't caught and interrogated, this is nothing but false accusation and violence from our side. You understand that don't you?"

Greifer showed a grave look. But Coral also didn't concede at all. He retorted back with a cool tone.

Based from his dignified attitude, it wasn't hard to imagine that this young man whose appearance looked like a girl was also hiding an equal strength with Greifer.

"Keh! I got it already honor student-sama. Aa-aa, that's why I hate you."

Greifer spat out as though he lost interest before he sheathed his sword and dispelled his armor.

Coral who saw that then approached the clock tower where Lux crashed onto.

"Are you all right? Any injury‐"

"No. I'm still fine, more or less."

Lux told so to Coral who was holding out his hand toward Lux worriedly. Lux then went down to the ground with his own strength.

Certainly he didn't have any serious injury or damage.

But, it was only him escaping such thing with a paper-thin difference, if Coral was late several second, he didn't know what would happen to him.

"By all right, this matter have to be reported and discussed with the judge panel of the All-Dragon Battle and, but……"

Coral also went down and dispelled his armor. Then he muttered that with an awkward look.

By all rights, the selection members for the All-Dragon Battle from each country weren't permitted to battle each other outside the arena. In the case that rule was broken, the offender would be banned from participating‐or depending on the situation, the represented country would also be disqualified.

Because this time it was Greifer who inititated the fight, that rule should be applied to him, but Lux shook his head.

"No. It's fine if we treat this matter as never happened. I don't know about the detail, but it seemed that the new kingdom's guard attacked your member first……. I too don't want to make this into a big problem."

"It also cannot be like that. At the very least we have to check whether you are injured or not‐if you tell me where is the capital's hospital is located,

I'll accompany you there."

"Oooi, honor student. Since when you became the new kingdom's aide

huh?"

"You just shut up over there."

Coral scolded with red face when Greifer pointed out with casual tone.

Lux was thankful for Coral's consideration, but Lux too didn't intend to prolong this matter for more than this.

"I'm really all right. Rather than that, our side will also investigate about the matter in question, so for today‐"

"……I guess. It will be a big day for both of us tomorrow, we too has already reported to the other guard just now, so‐later."

When Lux said that, Coral bowed in thanks and walked away.

Even though he had come until this far outskirt, he didn't leave using Drag-Ride was to avoid even further commotion than this.

At the sky, several Drag-Knights from the military were already circling around because they heard the commotion.

"Then, I'm going home too. I got a bit of bone to pick with you and this country, but let's settle it next time. It's a waste to finish you with this kind of half-baked battle."

Greifer grinned while saying that before he left.

"……Fuu."

The time that was like a storm passed and Lux was finally liberated.

There was no curfew at the inn they were reserving, but he didn't want to worry everyone, so he hurriedly went back.

Lux dragged his body that was heavy from fatigue and somehow managed to return until the inn. There, Airi was standing in front of the door with a stole wrapped on her shoulders.

"Uwa……"

Those reproachful eyes staring at him caused Lux to raise his voice reflexively.

"'Uwa……' , it's me who want to say that. What were you doing fighting like that? What a no good Nii-san as usual."

Airi immediately replied with an exasperated tone.

Most likely she explained the situation to Relie and asked her to dispatch the army's guard to reinforce Lux. After that she was waiting for Lux's return here.

"No but, I was pursued……and I couldn't shake him off."

"Wouldn't it be fine if Nii-san ran away to a place with a lot of people or to a military facility? ……Well, though knowing Nii-san you must have escaped to the direction of the redeveloped district where there is no people so that no one will get dragged into it."

"…………"

Everything was seen through so Lux couldn't even say anything in his defense.

"Let's go inside quickly. You will catch cold if you stay wet like that."

Airi opened the door and urged Lux to come in. Lux obeyed her meekly and followed behind her.

Part 11

"Eh!? You knew the true identity of the culprit? The one who attacked the selection member of Wanheim Principality‐"

"Please lower your voice Nii-san. It will become complicated again if someone heard it by any chance."

Lux wiped his body that was wet from rain, drank a hot tea, and warmed his cold body.

After that, he entered the double room that he shared with Airi in order to sleep. But the first word he heard right after entering inside caused Lux to raise his voice unconsciously.

The incident not long ago that became the origin of the dispute.

A Drag Knight of the new kingdom attacked the inn of Wanheim

Principality. Airi said that she knew the true identity of the attacker.

"Yes, that kind of skillful rampage method is impossible. Besides, it seems that officer is quite the veteran, and when his Drag-Ride was inspected there wasn't any abnormality."

A rampage that happened in an impossible timing and an assault that occurred because of that.

"I see."

If a conclusion had to be spoken, that officer himself might be a spy from somewhere.

"……Yes."

Airi quietly talked to Lux inside the bedroom that had its lighting turned off.

Lux too noticed it.

Yoruka's Divine Drag-Ride that he had already told to Airi too‐Yato no Kami.

The ability of Spell Code, the Divine Raimen that dominated and controlled other people's Drag-Ride.

If it was with her strength and skill‐certainly she could easily cause this kind of incident.

(But……I don't understand. Is this, really Yoruka's work?)

The piled up fatigue was gradually robbing him of his ability to think.

And then, Lux fell asleep.

Chapter 3: The Girls' Reward

Part 1

The next day, the international tournament‐All-Dragon Battle's first day was finally held.

The place was the Drag-Ride arena nearby the castle.

The scale was even larger than the academy's practice ground. A great number of citizens and nobles were gathering there.

It was scheduled for three days. In order to limit the Drag-Knights' fatigue to the minimum, there would be one day of rest in between. The tournament was divided to the first half in the first day and the later half in the second day and it was carried out under special rule.

The tournament this time was a round robin event that was performed by the seven participating country.

Three battle in the first half, and three battle in the later half. A total of six battles would be carried out.

The competition rule against a country was a maximum of the three matches, the one who took the first two victory in two matches won the battle. It was fundamentally based on the rule of the capital's tournament.

There was two kind of matches, a one-on-one individual battle, and a twoon-two pair battle. The side that settled two wins first would win at that time.

In the case the result was one win and one loss, both camps would choose a member who still hadn't fought and the last individual battle would decide it.

It was only after all the members had performed once that the team could choose once more between all their members.

Therefore the comprehensive strength of the team was stressed here. It was a system where it would be hard to be victorious by depending on the great effort of a single powerful member.

When the members of the new kingdom gathered inside the waiting room in the arena, the leader of Syvalles Celis stood in front of everyone.

"The three battles today will be against religious country Ymir, Turkimes

Confederation, and Blackened Kingdom. About the first battle against Ymir, I believe we will carry it out without our four Divine Drag-Ride users as arranged."

"Aa, if I'm not mistaken this is what you called throwing a match right……?"

Tillfur of Tria who heard that spoke sounding somewhat dejectedly.

"No. It's what you call a strategic bargaining. Or rather, please don't bring up again the matter that has been decided from previous discussion."

Noct immediately retorted and lightly clapped on Tillfur's back.

The new kingdom ide ended up borrowing Krulcifer who was a prominent Drag-Knight from their allied country Ymir.

Therefore, it was the moral principle for the new kingdom to not put Krulcifer in the first battle against Ymir, and they also couldn't show a stance of doing their all to win by investing their other Divine Drag-Ride user.

Because of such reason it was decided to enter the users of general purpose Drag-Ride only against religious country Ymir.

In this aspect, it was the instruction that came from the capital government's strategic bargaining rather than the selection members themselves, so there was also an implicit understanding part in it.

And then Tillfur was planned to enter the first match, the individual match of this battle.

"But of course, you don't mind if we actually won this battle right, captaindono?"

When Sharis said that, Celis nodded with a serious look and,

Part 2

The case with Greifer that occurred yesterday, and Tiamat's rampage that occurred today.

Part 4

And then the next morning.

The country founding anniversary of the new kingdom finally began.

At the All-Dragon Battle's schedule, today was the second day that was for a resting day. The participants were basically free whether to rest or to look around the festival.

Lux received a request from Krulcifer to 'go around the festival together' as the reward for finishing her assignment at the training camp.

Krulcifer was already waiting when he headed to the entrance of the inn where they were staying.

Krulcifer wasn't wearing her usual cool smile, but she looked slightly awkward with a complicated smile.

In the middle of All-Dragon Battle, there was a rule that the participating selection members had to wear their uniform when going outside, so the two of them also wore their uniform, but Lux's concern didn't lie there.

"This, I'm sorry Krulcifer-san. I never thought, that it would become like this‐"

'Eh, ah, right……. That's‐fine though.'

Lux was shook up by Philuffy who said that straightforwardly with her serious face and carefree tone stayed unchanging. His cheeks reddened while he consented.

Since the past the two of them had played together many times, but this was the first time she called it a 'date', so he somehow felt embarrassed.

Part 5

A large mansion located in the capital‐Moon Lamp Mansion. It was the first time Lux entered inside it.

That facility which was mainly used for the party of nobles was divided into three floors. It had a bar that also offered meal, and a lounge with chic atmosphere.

Its main attraction was the dance hall that was decorated with gorgeous furniture and chandelier with beautiful craftsmanship.

People could also borrow outfit there although it would take some money. It was a famous social meeting place that anyone would show their face at least once there if they were a noble at the capital.

Especially at this period when the country founding anniversary was on going, the venue was really crowded and enveloped in hustle and bustle since the daytime.

After lightly viewing the bar and the lounge, both Lux and Krulcifer rented outfit for themselves and changed into it.

When Lux who changed into a white ceremonial clothes was waiting at the dance hall, the door of the changing room opened and Krulcifer in dress appearance made her appearance.

"I've made you wait. I chose a slightly reserved piece however‐what do you think?"

Lux spontaneously held his breath after taking a glance at her appearance.

She was beautiful.

She was wearing a smooth jet black dress that made the whiteness of her

skin that was like powdered snow became prominent.

The area around her neck that was wrapped with black choker opened widely until her chest, showing the curve of that slender stature even more beautifully and charmingly.

Her long blue hair that was like silk was gently bundled with hair clip and ribbon, spreading downward in a gentle arc.

His feeling was paralyzed because he had gotten used at seeing her from nearby daily, but when she dressed up properly like this, he felt further from her a beauty that was in different dimension.

"Suddenly choosing a dress on the spot is really difficult isn't it? It's good that I can somehow make it look appropriate but‐"
